<div><a name="s41F67703753D55D395C07B977C11B693"></a></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><div style="padding-left:0px;text-indent:0px;line-height:normal;padding-top:10px;text-align:-moz-right;"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;width:99.609375%;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;margin-left:auto;margin-right:0;"><tr><td colspan="3"></td></tr><tr><td style="width:34%;"></td><td style="width:33%;"></td><td style="width:33%;"></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="overflow:hidden;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="overflow:hidden;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Press Release</font></div><div style="text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Exhibit 99.1</font></div></td></tr></table></div></div></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:232%;text-align:center;font-size:15pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:15pt;font-weight:bold;">Acuity Brands Reports Fiscal 2020 Second Quarter Results</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:17px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">ATLANTA, April 2, 2020 - Acuity Brands, Inc. (NYSE: AYI) (&#8220;Company&#8221;) today announced results for the second quarter ended on February 29, 2020.  Second quarter net sales were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$824 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">3.5%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared with the year-ago period. Gross profit margin of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">41.7%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">260</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;basis points from the prior-year period.  Operating profit margin of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">9.9%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;declined </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">130</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;basis points and adjusted operating profit margin of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">12.3%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;declined </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">90</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;basis points from the prior-year period.  Diluted earnings per share (EPS) of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.44</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;declined </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">13.8%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and adjusted diluted EPS of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.84</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;declined </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">7.5%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from the prior-year period.  For the six months ended February 29, 2020, cash flow from operations increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$26 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">14.0%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, from the prior-year period to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$215 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Neil Ashe, President and Chief Executive Officer of Acuity Brands, commented, &#8220;Results for the second quarter were a combination of continuing trends with some signs of improvement.  We are embarking on the next generation of Acuity Brands while at the same time we are dealing with the shocks caused by the COVID-19 pandemic.  We are focused on the health and well-being of our associates while aggressively managing the risks and opportunities that the COVID-19 shocks present to the Company.  We enter this period with a strong balance sheet and a strong team.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:26px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Fiscal 2020 Second Quarter Results</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:17px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Fiscal 2020 second quarter net sales of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$824 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">3.5%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared with the prior-year period due primarily to a </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">7%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;decrease in volume, partially offset by a contribution from acquisitions of approximately </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">3%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, and a </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;net favorable change in price and mix of products sold (&#8220;price/mix&#8221;).  Management estimates that price/mix was impacted by a favorable shift in sales channel mix, partially offset by an unfavorable mix of products sold.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Gross profit for the second quarter of fiscal 2020 increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$10 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$344 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$334 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the prior-year period due primarily to the contribution from acquisitions, lower costs for certain inputs, and favorable price/mix.  These increases were partially offset by lower sales volume and increased tariffs.  Fiscal 2020 second quarter gross profit margin of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">41.7%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">260</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;basis points compared with the prior-year period&#8217;s gross profit margin. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Selling, distribution, and administrative (&#8220;SD&amp;A&#8221;) expenses for the second quarter of fiscal 2020 totaled </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$261 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$23 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or approximately </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">9.8%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, compared with the prior-year period.  The increase in SD&amp;A expense in the second quarter was due primarily to the addition of costs from acquired businesses, increased commissions, higher professional fees, and higher variable incentive compensation.  Adjusted SD&amp;A expenses for the second quarter of fiscal 2020 totaled </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$242 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$20 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">8.9%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared with the prior-year period.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Operating profit for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$81 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">9.9%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales, compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$96 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">11.2%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales, for the prior-year period.  The decrease in operating profit was due to higher SD&amp;A expenses and increased special charges, partially offset by higher gross profit.  Adjusted operating profit for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;quarter of fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$102 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">12.3%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales, compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$112 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">13.2%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales, for the prior-year period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:26px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Year-to-Date Results</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:17px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Net sales for the first six months of fiscal 2020 were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.66 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.79 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;reported for the prior-year period, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$128 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">7.2%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.  Operating profit for the first </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months of fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$165 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$212 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the prior-year period, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$47 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">22.3%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Operating profit margin for the first </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">six</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;months of fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">200</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;basis points to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">9.9%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">11.9%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net sales in the year-ago period.  Net income for the first six months of fiscal 2020 was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$114 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$32 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">21.7%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$146 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the Acuity Brands achieves growth through the development of innovative new products and services.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Through the Acuity Business System, the Company achieves customer-focused efficiencies that allow the Company to increase market share and deliver superior returns. style="line-height:120%;padding-top:17px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:17px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">This news release includes the following non-Generally Accepted Accounting Principles (GAAP) financial measures: &#8220;adjusted gross profit,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted gross profit margin,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted SD&amp;A expenses,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted SD&amp;A expenses as a percent of net sales,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted operating profit,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted operating profit margin,&#8221; &#8220;adjusted net income,&#8221; and &#8220;adjusted diluted EPS.&#8221;  These non-GAAP financial measures are provided to enhance the reader's overall understanding of the Company's current financial performance and prospects for the future.  Specifically, management believes that these non-GAAP measures provide useful information to investors by excluding or adjusting items for manufacturing inefficiencies, acquisition-related items, amortization of acquired intangible assets, share-based payment expense, and special charges associated with continued efforts to streamline the organization to integrate acquisitions.  Management typically adjusts for these items for internal reviews of performance and uses the above non-GAAP measures for baseline comparative operational analysis, decision making, and other activities.  Management believes these non-GAAP measures provide greater comparability and enhanced visibility into the Company&#8217;s results of operations as well as comparability with many of its peers, especially those companies focused more on technology and software.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:9px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Non-GAAP financial measures included in this news release should be considered in addition to, and not as a substitute for or superior to, results prepared in accordance with GAAP.  The most directly comparable GAAP measures for adjusted gross profit and adjusted gross profit margin are &#8220;gross profit&#8221; and &#8220;gross profit margin,&#8221; respectively, which include the impact of manufacturing inefficiencies and acquisition-related items. The most directly comparable GAAP measure for adjusted SD&amp;A expenses and adjusted SD&amp;A expenses as a percent of net sales is &#8220;SD&amp;A expenses&#8221; and &#8220;SD&amp;A expenses as a percent of net sales,&#8221; which include amortization of acquired intangible assets, share-based payment expense, and acquisition-related items. The most directly comparable GAAP measures for adjusted operating profit and adjusted operating profit margin are &#8220;operating profit&#8221; and &#8220;operating profit margin,&#8221; respectively, which include the impact of manufacturing inefficiencies, acquisition-related items, amortization of acquired intangible assets, share-based payment expense, and special charges. The most directly comparable GAAP measures for adjusted net income and adjusted diluted EPS are &#8220;net income&#8221; and &#8220;diluted EPS,&#8221; respectively, which include the impact of manufacturing inefficiencies, acquisition-related items, amortization of acquired intangible assets, share-based payment expense, and special charges. A reconciliation of each measure to the most directly comparable GAAP measure is available in this news release. The Company&#8217;s non-GAAP financial measures may not be comparable to similarly titled non-GAAP financial measures used by other companies, have limitations as an analytical tool, and should not be considered in isolation or as a substitute for GAAP financial measures.</font></div><div><br></div><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font
